[30;1m124 | [0m[35mCompile Chipmunk[0m
[30;1m125 | [0m[35m================[0m
[30;1m126 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m127 | [0m[35mPymunk is built on top of the c library Chipmunk. It uses CFFI to interface[0m
[30;1m128 | [0m[35mwith the Chipmunk library file. Because of this Chipmunk has to be compiled[0m
[30;1m129 | [0m[35mtogether with Pymunk as an extension module. [0m
[30;1m130 | [0m[35m[0m

[30;1m40 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m41 | [0m[35mPymunk is an easy-to-use pythonic 2D physics library that can be used whenever [0m
[30;1m42 | [0m[35myou need 2D rigid body physics from Python. Perfect when you need 2D physics [0m
[30;1m43 | [0m[35min your game, demo or simulation! It is built on top of the very [0m
[30;1m44 | [0m[35mcapable 2D physics library `Chipmunk2D <http://chipmunk-physics.net>`_.[0m
[30;1m45 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m46 | [0m[35mThe first version was released in 2007 and Pymunk is still actively developed [0m
